###########################
# USA Events By herkles
###########################

add_namespace = ustates

country_event = { # Start up Event
	id = ustates.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.1" }
	title = ustates.1.t
	desc = ustates.1.d
	picture = congress
	
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.1.a
	}
}

### Lead up to the Civil War ###
country_event = { # Black Monday hits America
	id = ustates.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.2" }
	title = ustates.2.t
	desc = ustates.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_run_on_the_banks

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.2.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_great_depression }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = USA_great_depression
				add_idea = USA_black_monday
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = USA_black_monday
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HON = {
				country_event = {
					id = honduras.100
					days = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Coalition Ticket?
	id = ustates.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.3" }
	title = ustates.3.t
	desc = ustates.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Form the Coalition
		name = ustates.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_AVOIDED
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = 3
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = USA_coalition_long
				name = USA_coalition
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.8
				days = 85
				} #Nominating Quentin Roosevelt
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.20
				days = 110
				} #Death of Big Bill Haywood
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.4
				days = 125
				} #Southern Democrats take umbrage
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.5
				days = 150
				} #Democrats v Republicans
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.6
				days = 175
				} #Coalition Rally
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.21
				days = 190
				} #Fighting between AFP and SPA politicians
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.19
				days = 200
				} #Huey Long Speaks
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.7
				days = 215
				} #Republicans v Olson's people
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.9
				days = 235
				} #Indian Citizenship Act
		}
	}
	option = { # Don't form the coalition
		name = ustates.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TXS_independence
						option = TXS_INDEPENDENCE_GUARENTEE
					}
				}
					
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.11
				days = 56
				} #Increasing Radicalizing
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.12
				days = 95
				} #Olson's people flock to the SPA
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.20
				days = 110
				} #Death of Big Bill Haywood
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.13
				days = 115
				} #Democrat voters align with the AFP
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.14
				days = 153
				} #MacArthur speaks to Hoover
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.15
				days = 185
				} #The Battle of the Overpass
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.21
				days = 190
				} #Fighting between AFP and SPA politicians
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.19
				days = 200
				} #Huey Long Speaks
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.16
				days = 215
				} #Representatives Retiring
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.17
				days = 235
				} #Fighting between the SPA and AFP
		}
	}
}


### Coalition stuff
country_event = { # Southern Democrats take umbrage
	id = ustates.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.4" }
	title = ustates.4.t
	desc = ustates.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = { # Let them Complain
		name = ustates.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_AVOIDED
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Force a compromise
		name = ustates.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = { # Democrats v Republicans
	id = ustates.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.5" }
	title = ustates.5.t
	desc = ustates.5.d
	picture = USA_july4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = { # side with the democrats
		name = ustates.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_AVOIDED
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = -1
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
	option = { # Force a compromise
		name = ustates.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # side with the republicans
		name = ustates.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_COMPROMISE_WITH_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_AVOIDED
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_coalition_strength
				value = -1
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Coalition falls apart!
	id = ustates.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.10" }
	title = ustates.10.t
	desc = ustates.10.d
	picture = GFX_USA_Riots

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_coalition_strength
			value < 1
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.10.a
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -100
		clr_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = USA_social_democrat_party_long
				name = USA_social_democrat_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = USA_social_liberal_party_long
				name = USA_social_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = USA_market_liberal_party_long
				name = USA_market_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = USA_social_conservative_party_long
				name = USA_social_conservative_party
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_AFP_gains_strength
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 1 }
		}
	}
}


### No Coalition Stuff
country_event = { # Increasing Radicalizing
	id = ustates.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.11" }
	title = ustates.11.t
	desc = ustates.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_iww_demonstration

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = USA_no_coalition_party
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_election_1936_flag }
	}

	option = { # radicalization
		name = ustates.11.a
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_AFP_gains_strength
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Bounce event to determine success
	id = ustates.86

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SUCCESS
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
		    factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_civil_war
					option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_THREE_SIDES
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long }
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long
				set_country_flag = USA_assassinated_long
				news_event = ustates.87
				country_event = { id = ustates.89 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_reed
				set_country_flag = USA_assassinated_reed
				news_event = ustates.88
				country_event = { id = ustates.90 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = FAILURE
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
		    factor = 0
		    OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_KILL_LONG_USA_VS_CSA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = USA_civil_war
						option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_KILL_REED_USA_VS_TEX
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long }
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_long
				set_country_flag = USA_fails_to_kill_long_flag
				add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 2 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = USA_Charles_Curtis_hog_mli }
					country_event = amcivwar.11
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_idea = USA_John_Nance_Garner_hog_sco }
					country_event = amcivwar.14
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_idea = USA_Alf_Landon_hog_sli }
					country_event = amcivwar.17
				}
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_assassinating_reed
				set_country_flag = USA_fails_to_kill_reed_flag
				add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 2 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = USA_Charles_Curtis_hog_mli }
					country_event = amcivwar.12
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_idea = USA_John_Nance_Garner_hog_sco }
					country_event = amcivwar.15
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_idea = USA_Alf_Landon_hog_sli }
					country_event = amcivwar.18
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The great Migration
	id = ustates.134
	title = ustates.134.t
	desc = ustates.134.d
	picture = GFX_USA_reconstruction

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag
		OR = {
			country_exists = CAL
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				has_democratic_government = yes
				any_owned_state = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.134"
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CAL }
			CAL = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NEE }
			NEE = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAN = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # kill them
		name = ustates.134.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration1
			days = 90
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_stability = 0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.135
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Let them go
		name = ustates.134.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_war_support = -0.02
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration2
			days = 50
		}
		add_manpower = -2500
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.135
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.164" }
	title = ustates.164.t
	desc = ustates.164.d
	picture = GFX_USA_reconstruction1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Nationalize just the tracks
		name = ustates.164.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Nationalize both cars and track
		name = ustates.164.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

country_event = { # Canada Agrees
	id = ustates.166
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.166" }
	title = ustates.166.t
	desc = ustates.166.d
	picture = congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = ustates.166.a
		276 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		486 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = CAN }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		796 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# End to the Coalition ticket
	id = ustates.168
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.168" }
	title = ustates.168.t
	desc = ustates.168.d
	picture = congress

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		date > 1939.05.14
		has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {# The end of the Coalition party
		name = ustates.168.a
		clr_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = USA_social_democrat_party_long
				name = USA_social_democrat_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = USA_social_liberal_party_long
				name = USA_social_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = USA_market_liberal_party_long
				name = USA_market_liberal_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = USA_social_conservative_party_long
				name = USA_social_conservative_party
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

country_event = { # Floyd Olson Passes Away
	id = ustates.185
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.185" }
	title = ustates.185.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.185.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Floyd Olson"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.185.d.senator
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Floyd Olson"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_USA_curtis

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ustates.185.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Floyd Olson"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -15
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Quentin Roosevelt"
			desc = "POLITICS_QUENTIN_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_USA_Quentin_Roosevelt.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			traits = {
				appeaser
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { # Henry Wallace
				name = "Henry Wallace"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {
					tenacious_negotiator
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_hog_sli
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.185.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Floyd Olson"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -5
	}
}


### 1940 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1940 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.200" }
	title = ustates.200.t
	desc = ustates.200.d
	picture = congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = ustates.200.a
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_progressive_primary_wallace
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Republican Primary
	id = ustates.201
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.201" }
	title = ustates.201.t
	picture = congress

	desc = {
		text = ustates.201.d.avoided
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Alf Landon"
				}
			}
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.201.d.landon
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Alf Landon"
			}
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.201.d.not_elected
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # nominate Quentin Roosevelt
		name = ustates.201.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						ruling_only = yes
						name = "Alf Landon"
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_roosevelt
	}
	option = { # re-nominate Alf Landon
		name = ustates.201.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Alf Landon"
			}
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_landon
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.202
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.202" }
	title = ustates.202.t
	desc = { # Democratic Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.202.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.202.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
		}
	}
	picture = congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Wendell Willkie (liberal)
		name = ustates.202.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # John Nance Garner
		name = ustates.202.b
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_garner
	}
	option = { # Harry F. Byrd
		name = ustates.202.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Douglas Macarthur
		name = ustates.202.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Election
	id = ustates.203
	title = ustates.203.t
	desc = ustates.203.d.civil_war_happened
	picture = congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.203"
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { # Henry Wallace
				name = "Henry Wallace"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {
					tenacious_negotiator
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_landon }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Alf Landon"
					desc = "POLITICS_ALF_LANDON_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Alf_Landon_KR.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						economic_reformer
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Quentin Roosevelt
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_landon }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Quentin Roosevelt"
					desc = "POLITICS_QUENTIN_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Quentin_Roosevelt.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						appeaser
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Wendell Willkie"
					desc = "POLITICS_WENDELL_WILLKIE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Wendell_Willkie_KR.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						appeaser
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Nance Garner"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_NANCE_GARNER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_John_Nance_Garner.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						strict_austerity_adherent
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry F. Byrd"
					desc = "POLITICS_HARRY_BYRD_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Harry_F_Byrd.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						backroom_backstabber
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Douglas MacArthur
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Douglas MacArthur"
					desc = "POLITICS_DOUGLAS_MACARTHUR_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_civ_douglas_macarthur.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						war_industrialist
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican
		name = ustates.203.a
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_republican
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Alf Landon
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_landon }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Alf_Landon_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
			}
			if = { # Quentin Roosevelt
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_republican_primary_landon }
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.175
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.204
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.205
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = ustates.203.b
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.20
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.20
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Wendell Willkie
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Wendell_Willkie_hog_mli
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
					USA_Roy_Dikeman_Chapin_Sr_eco_mli
					USA_Alben_W_Barkley_sec_mli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.176
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.177
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			if = { # Harry F. Byrd
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Harry_F_Byrd_hog_sco
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
					USA_William_Daniel_Leahy_eco_sco
					USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
				}
			}
			if = { # Douglas MacArthur
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_sco
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
					USA_William_Daniel_Leahy_eco_sco
					USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
				}
			}
			if = { # John Nance Garner
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_willkie
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_byrd
						has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur
					}
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_John_Nance_Garner_hog_sco
					USA_Cordell_Hull_for_mli
					USA_Alfred_Emanuel_Smith_eco_mli
					USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.171
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.172
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.204
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.205
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Progressive
		name = ustates.203.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				USA_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
				USA_Hugh_Simons_Gibson_for_sde
				USA_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
				USA_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.179
				days = 60
				random = 15840
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.204
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.205
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.206
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
}


### 1944 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1944 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.204
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.204" }
	title = ustates.204.t
	picture = congress

	desc = { # Progressive Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.204.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.204.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = ustates.204.a
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_wallace
	}
	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.204.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Republican Primary
	id = ustates.205
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.205" }
	title = ustates.205.t
	picture = congress

	desc = { # Republican Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.205.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = { # Republican Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.205.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # nominate Thomas Dewey
		name = ustates.205.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
	}
	option = { # nominate Quentin Roosevelt
		name = ustates.205.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_liberal }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_roosevelt
	}
	option = { # Re-nominate the President
		name = ustates.205.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Democrat Primary
	id = ustates.206
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.206" }
	title = ustates.206.t
	picture = congress

	desc = { # Democratic Party has the Presidency
		text = ustates.206.d.president
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democratic Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.206.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Richard Russell Jr.
		name = ustates.206.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_russell
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Alben W. Barkley
		name = ustates.206.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # James E. Murray
		name = ustates.206.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
			value = -1
		}
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # re-nominate the President
		name = ustates.206.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Wendell Willkie"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.170 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry F. Byrd"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Douglas MacArthur"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_conservative_democratic_power
				value = 1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = USA_liberal_democratic_power
				value = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.169 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Election
	id = ustates.207
	title = ustates.207.t
	desc = ustates.207.d
	picture = congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.207"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Philip La Follette"
					desc = "POLITICS_PHILIP_LA_FOLLETTE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Philip_La_Follette.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						reluctant_interventionist
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry Wallace"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						great_survivor
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Thomas Dewey"
					desc = "POLITICS_THOMAS_DEWEY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Thomas_Dewey_KR.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						great_survivor
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Quentin Roosevelt"
					desc = "POLITICS_QUENTIN_ROOSEVELT_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Quentin_Roosevelt.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						appeaser
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "James E. Murray"
					desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_MURRAY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_James_Murray.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Alben W. Barkley"
					desc = "POLITICS_ALBEN_BARKLEY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Alben_Barkley.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						silent_workhorse
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Richard Russell Jr."
					desc = "POLITICS_RICHARD_RUSSELL_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Richard_Russell_Jr.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						nationalist_symbol
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Progressive
		name = ustates.207.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Philip La Follette
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Philip_La_Follette_hog_sde
					USA_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
					USA_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
					USA_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
				}
			}
			if = { # Henry Wallace
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_progressive_primary_follette }
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
					USA_Hugh_Simons_Gibson_for_sde
					USA_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
					USA_Elmer_Austin_Benson_sec_sde
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.179
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Republican
		name = ustates.207.b
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_republican
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Thomas Dewey
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Thomas_Dewey_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.184
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			if = { # Quentin Roosevelt
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_dewey
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_republican_primary_president
					}
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.175
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = ustates.207.c
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_russell }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
					has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = market_liberal
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		}
		else = {
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_20 = yes
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # James E. Murray
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_James_E_Murray_hog_mli
					USA_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Alben_W_Barkley_sec_mli
				}
			}
			if = { # Alben W. Barkley
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Alben_W_Barkley_hog_mli
					USA_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Robert_Ferdinand_Wagner_I_sec_mli
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.182
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}
			if = { # Richard Russell Jr.
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_murray
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_barkley
						has_country_flag = USA_1944_democratic_primary_president
					}
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Richard_Russell_Jr_hog_sco
					USA_James_Watson_Gerard_Jr_for_sco
					USA_Dean_Gooderham_Acheson_for_sco
					USA_Martin_Dies_Jr_sec_sco
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ustates.183
					days = 60
					random = 15840
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.209
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.210
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.211
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.212
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
}


### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1948 Progressive Party
	id = ustates.209
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.209" }
	title = ustates.209.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.209.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1940
		text = ustates.209.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.209.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.209.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_progressive_primary_folette
	}
	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = ustates.209.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_progressive_primary_taylor
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = ustates.209.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_progressive }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_progressive_primary_president
	}
}

		}
	}

	desc = { # democrats Party won the presidency just last time

		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election

			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_truman
	}
	option = { # William Averell Harriman
		name = ustates.211.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = market_liberal }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_democrat }
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}

	}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_election_democrat }

					USA_Quentin_Roosevelt_II_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
			}
			if = { # Earl Warren
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_warren }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Earl_Warren_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles L. McNary
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_republican_primary_mcnary }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Charles_L_McNary_hog_sli
					USA_John_Bassett_Moore_for_sli
					USA_Charles_Edison_eco_sli
					USA_Charles_Douglas_Jackson_sec_sli
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.214
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.215
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.216
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.217
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Liberal Democrat
		name = ustates.213.c
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_election_liberal
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Harry Truman
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_truman }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_Harry_Truman_hog_mli
					USA_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Robert_Ferdinand_Wagner_I_sec_mli
				}
			}
			if = { # William Averell Harriman
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_liberal_democrat_primary_harriman }
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					USA_William_Averell_Harriman_hog_mli
					USA_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_mli
					USA_Daniel_Calhoun_Roper_eco_mli
					USA_Robert_Ferdinand_Wagner_I_sec_mli
				}
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.214
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.215
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.216
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ustates.217
				days = 1304
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Conservative Democrat
		name = ustates.213.e
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1948_election_conservative
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative

### 1952 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1952 Progressive Primary
	id = ustates.214
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.214" }
	title = ustates.214.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = ustates.214.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1944
		text = ustates.214.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = ustates.214.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
		}
	}
	picture = congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Philip La Follette
		name = ustates.214.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_folette
	}
	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = ustates.214.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive }
				has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_taylor
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = ustates.214.c
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_progressive
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_progressive }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_president
	}
}

		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election

			has_country_flag = USA_1948_election_republican
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_1944_election_republican }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_republican_primary_president
	}
}

country_event = { # 1952 election
	id = ustates.218
	title = ustates.218.t
	desc = ustates.218.d
	picture = congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1936_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = USA_had_1948_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election }
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.218"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Philip La Follette
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_folette }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Philip La Follette"
					desc = "POLITICS_PHILIP_LA_FOLLETTE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Philip_La_Follette.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						reluctant_interventionist
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Glen H. Taylor
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_progressive_primary_taylor }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Glen H. Taylor"
					desc = "POLITICS_GLEN_TAYLOR_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Glen_Taylor.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						figurehead_president
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John W. Bricker
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_republican_primary_bricker }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John W. Bricker"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_BRICKER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_John_W_Bricker.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						strict_austerity_adherent
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Harold Stassen
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_republican_primary_stassen }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harold Stassen"
					desc = "POLITICS_HAROLD_STASSEN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Harold_Stassen.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Dwight D. Eisenhower
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_eisenhower }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Dwight D. Eisenhower"
					desc = "POLITICS_DWIGHT_EISENHOWER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Dwight_Eisenhower.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						great_war_hero
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Adlai Stevenson
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_liberal_primary_stevenson }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = " Adlai Stevenson"
					desc = "POLITICS_ADLAI_STEVENSON_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_Adlai_Stevenson.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = {
						tenacious_negotiator
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John Sparkman
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_conservative_primary_sparkman }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Sparkman"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_SPARKMAN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_John_Sparkman.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						quartermaster_general
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # James Eastland
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1952_conservative_primary_eastland }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "James Eastland"
					desc = "POLITICS_HARRY_CAIN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_USA_James_Eastland.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = {
						divided_interests
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Progressive
		name = ustates.218.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_progressives_exist
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_had_1952_election
		set_country_flag = USA_1952_election_progressive
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = {

			}

				tag = YUC
			}

				factor = 0.85

					tag = MEX
					tag = CEN
				}
			}
		}

			target = USA
			modifier = USA_joined_league

					value = 200

					type = support

					tag = MEX

			}

				factor = 3
				tag = YUC

		}

			target = FROM

country_event = { # Remove the League idea
	id = ustates.254
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.254" }
	title = ustates.254.t
	desc = ustates.254.d
	picture = GFX_SWI_diplomacy2

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_league_of_america_1
			has_idea = USA_league_of_america_2
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = USA }
			is_major = yes
			has_war_with = USA
			AND = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
			}
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.254.a
		clr_country_flag = USA_sent_league_invite
		clr_country_flag = USA_received_industrial_aid
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_of_america_1 }
			remove_ideas = USA_league_of_america_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_of_america_2 }
			remove_ideas = USA_league_of_america_2
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = USA_joined_league
		}
		USA = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = USA_joined_league
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_guaranteed_by = USA }
			USA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { gives_military_access_to = USA }
			USA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = -1
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = protect
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Change League idea
	id = ustates.255
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.255" }
	title = ustates.255.t
	desc = ustates.255.d
	picture = GFX_SWI_diplomacy2

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_completed_focus = USA_cooperaton_treaties
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_idea = USA_league_head_1 }
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_1
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 1
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_idea = USA_league_head_2 }
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_2
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 9
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_idea = USA_league_head_3 }
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_3
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than

					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 1
						compare = less_than
					}

						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_head_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_2

					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 5
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_league_members
						value = 9
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_head_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_league_head_3
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 9
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_league_head_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = USA_league_head_1 }
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_league_members
					value = 5

				}
			}

		if = {

### Resistance Events ###
country_event = { # Socialist terrorism - factory sabotaged
	id = ustates.400
	title = ustates.400.t
	desc = ustates.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SRI_bombing

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA
			tag = CAL
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance1
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance2
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance3
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance4
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_core_of = CSA
				is_core_of = TEX
				is_core_of = CAL
			}
			industrial_complex > 0
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_idea = USA_socialist_resistance4
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.400"
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = USA
						is_core_of = CSA
						is_core_of = TEX
						is_core_of = CAL
					}
					industrial_complex > 0
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				save_event_target_as = attack_state
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.400.a
		add_stability = -0.01
		event_target:attack_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1.0
			}
			if = {
				limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = arms_factory
								damage = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
					50 = {}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { infrastructure > 3 }
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 2.0
							}
						}
					}
					50 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
					25 = {}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -3000
					}
				}
				50 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -1500
					}
				}
				25 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -500
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

							damage_building = {
								type = arms_factory
								damage = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
					50 = {}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { infrastructure > 3 }
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 2.0
							}
						}
					}
					50 = {
						event_target:attack_state = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 1.0
							}
						}
					}
					25 = {}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -3000
					}
				}
				50 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -1500
					}
				}
				25 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_manpower = -500
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ustates.506
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.506" }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = { #BILL PASSES
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				USA = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_longists_supported
						has_country_flag = USA_socialists_supported
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.507 hours = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = { #BILL FAILS
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = USA_establishment_supported
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = USA_establishment_supported
					has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				USA = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_establishment_supported }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				USA = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_establishment_supported }
					has_country_flag = USA_coalition_party
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.508 hours = 3 }
		}
	}
}

	id = ustates.526
	title = ustates.526.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_macarthur_speech

	desc = {
		text = ustates.526.d.reed
		trigger = { has_idea = USA_William_Haywood_hog_syn }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.526.d.long
		trigger = { has_idea = USA_Huey_Long_hog_ade }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.526.d.oldguard
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = USA_William_Haywood_hog_syn
				has_idea = USA_Huey_Long_hog_ade
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.526"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_macarthur_coup
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = USA_paternal_autocrat_military_junta
				name = USA_paternal_autocrat_military_junta
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Douglas MacArthur"
				desc = "POLITICS_DOUGLAS_MACARTHUR_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_USA_gen_douglas_macarthur.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				traits = {
					american_caesar
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.1150.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength2
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_AFP_gains_strength2
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AFP_strength value = 3 }
			add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 3 }
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_pau
				USA_John_William_Davis_for_pau
				USA_William_Harrison_Standley_eco_pau
				USA_William_Randolph_Hearst_Sr_sec_pau
			}
			country_event = { id = amcivwar.135 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			LEC = {
				country_event = { id = lecyankded.8 days = 1 }
			}
		}

	}
}

	desc = ustates.530.d

	option = {
		name = ustates.530.a #MacArthur did America a favor - we will rejoin, no questions asked
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = CAL_miss_ceasefire_name
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				USA = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
						has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.535 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.530.b #Yes, let them know we demand MacArthur be imprisoned first
		trigger = {
			USA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = CAL_rocky_ceasefire_name
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.532 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.530.c #We do not trust them, now or ever
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.531 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# PSA wants MacArthur Arrested First
country_event = {
	id = ustates.532
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.532" }
	title = ustates.532.t
	desc = ustates.532.d
	picture = GFX_PSA_golden_gate_crowd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = CAL }
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.532.a #For the good of America, let it be done
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_sco
				has_idea = USA_Douglas_MacArthur_hog_pau
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CAL = { has_country_flag = CAL_miss_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				CAL = { has_country_flag = CAL_rocky_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_macarthur }
			set_country_flag = USA_1940_democratic_primary_garner
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 56 }
			remove_unit_leader = 56
		}
		set_country_flag = Douglas_MacArthur_dead
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.10
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		CAL = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.534 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ustates.532.b #MacArthur is a hero - refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = USA_reed_was_president
					has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_considering_reunion
		add_political_power = 50
		CAL = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.533 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

			clr_country_flag = USA_considering_reunion

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				news_event = { id = ustates.536 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Authorize Fire Bombings?
	id = ustates.624
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ustates.624" }
	title = ustates.624.t
	desc = ustates.624.d
	picture = GFX_USA_bombing_run

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				has_war_with = TEX
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
			AND = {
				tag = TEX
				has_war_with = USA
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}

	option = {# Yes
		name = ustates.624.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				TEX = {
					exists = yes
				}
				NOT = { tag = TEX }
			}
			TEX = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_fire_bombings
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					exists = yes
				}
				NOT = { tag = USA }
			}
			USA = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_fire_bombings
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CSA = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			CSA = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_fire_bombings
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {# No
		name = ustates.624.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

	id = ustates.650

	desc = {
		text = ustates.650.AUS
		trigger = {
			tag = TEX
		}
	}

		text = ustates.650.PSA

			tag = CAL
		}
	}

			factor = 5
		}

				every_unit_leader = {

					set_nationality = CAL
				}

					set_nationality = CAL
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 958 } #McNair
					set_nationality = CAL
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 959 } #Fredendall
					set_nationality = CAL
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 965 } #Harding
					set_nationality = CAL
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 963 } #J.C.H. Lee
					set_nationality = CAL
				}
			}
		}
		if = {

					set_nationality = TEX

			}
